            function switch_li_bg(elm){
                var div = $(elm).parent().get(0);
                var li = $(div).parent().get(0)
                $(li).removeClass();
                if(elm.checked) $(li).addClass("item select");
                else $(li).addClass("item"); 
            }
            var s = '130';
            function item_compare(){
                var arr = new Array;
                $('input[name="C1"]:checked').each(function(){
                    arr.push(this.value);
                });
                if(arr.length > 0) window.open('http://search.books.com.tw/exep/prod_search_redir.php?key=%E7%B6%B2%E8%B7%AF%E7%A8%8B%E5%BC%8F%E8%A8%AD%E8%A8%88&area=mid_cmp&page=1&type=cmp&item='+arr.join(':'), 'wp1');
                else alert("尚未選擇商品！"); 
            }
            function item_putcart(){
                var arr = new Array;
                $('input[name="C1"]:checked').each(function(){
                    arr.push(this.value);
                });
                if(arr.length > 0) window.location = 'http://search.books.com.tw/exep/prod_search_redir.php?key=%E7%B6%B2%E8%B7%AF%E7%A8%8B%E5%BC%8F%E8%A8%AD%E8%A8%88&area=mid_cart&page=1&cart=1&pdf=1&item='+arr.join(':');
                else alert("尚未選擇購買商品！");  
            }
            function item_select(flag){
                $('input[name="C1"]').attr('checked',flag ? 'checked' : '');
                $(flag ? 'input[name="C1"]:checked' : 'input[name="C1"]').each(function(){
                    var div = $(this).parent().get(0);
                    var li = $(div).parent().get(0)
                    $(li).removeClass();
                    $(li).addClass(flag ? "item select" : "item");  
                });
            }
            function changePage(elm){
                var index = $(elm).val();
                window.location = "/exep/prod_search.php?cat=1&key=%E7%B6%B2%E8%B7%AF%E7%A8%8B%E5%BC%8F%E8%A8%AD%E8%A8%88&qsub=&qqsub=&page=" + index + "&sort=1&f=%3A%3A%3A%3A%3A%3A%3A%3A0%3A0%3A&c=";
            }
            function changeView(elm){
                window.location = "/exep/prod_search.php?cat=all&key=%E7%B6%B2%E8%B7%AF%E7%A8%8B%E5%BC%8F%E8%A8%AD%E8%A8%88&v=1";
            }
            function collapse(elm, type){
                window.location = "/exep/prod_search.php?cat=all&key=%E7%B6%B2%E8%B7%AF%E7%A8%8B%E5%BC%8F%E8%A8%AD%E8%A8%88&c=" + type + "&sort=1";
            }
            function advancedSearch(elm){
                var advancedForm = $("#advancedsearch");
                var rel = $(advancedForm).attr("rel");
                var key = encodeURI($("input[id='key'][name='key']").val());
                var catV = $("#query_type > option:selected").val();
                $(advancedForm).attr("action", "/exep/prod_search.php?cat=" + catV + "&key=" + key + "&c=&sort=1");
                var checked = $('#advancedsearch :checkbox').map(function() {
                	if($(this).attr('checked')) return 1;
                	else return 0;
				}).get(); 
                var price = [0, 0];
                if($.trim($('#price_min').val()).length) price[0] = $.trim($('#price_min').val());
                if($.trim($('#price_max').val()).length) price[1] = $.trim($('#price_max').val());
                var advancedList = $.merge(checked, price).join();
                 $.ajax({
                    type: 'get',
                    url: 'http://search.books.com.tw/exep/prod_search_mining.php',
                    data: 'area=' + rel + '&ref=' + act + '&adlist=' + advancedList,
                    error: function(data) {$(advancedForm).submit();},
                    success: function(data) {$(advancedForm).submit();}
                }); 
            }
            function reSearch(elm) {
                var fm = 0, bfm = 1, val = [];
                if($(elm).attr("id") == "fuzzySearch") fm = 1, bfm = 2;
                $("input[name='userTerm[]']:checked").each(function(i){
                    val[i] = $("label[for='" + $(this).attr('id') + "']").text();
                });
                if($.trim($("#customSearchText").val()) != '' && $.trim($("#customSearchText").val()) != "請輸入其它關鍵字") val.push($.trim($("#customSearchText").val()));
                if(val.length > 0) window.location = '/exep/prod_search.php?fm=' + fm + '&bfm=' + bfm + '&key=' + val.join(' ');
                else alert("請選擇關鍵字！");
            }

            function switch_li_bg(elm){
                var div = $(elm).parent().get(0);
                var li = $(div).parent().get(0)
                $(li).removeClass();
                if(elm.checked) $(li).addClass("item select");
                else $(li).addClass("item"); 
            }
            var s = '130';
            function item_compare(){
                var arr = new Array;
                $('input[name="C1"]:checked').each(function(){
                    arr.push(this.value);
                });
                if(arr.length > 0) window.open('http://search.books.com.tw/exep/prod_search_redir.php?key=%E7%B6%B2%E8%B7%AF%E7%A8%8B%E5%BC%8F%E8%A8%AD%E8%A8%88&area=mid_cmp&page=2&type=cmp&item='+arr.join(':'), 'wp1');
                else alert("尚未選擇商品！"); 
            }
            function item_putcart(){
                var arr = new Array;
                $('input[name="C1"]:checked').each(function(){
                    arr.push(this.value);
                });
                if(arr.length > 0) window.location = 'http://search.books.com.tw/exep/prod_search_redir.php?key=%E7%B6%B2%E8%B7%AF%E7%A8%8B%E5%BC%8F%E8%A8%AD%E8%A8%88&area=mid_cart&page=2&cart=1&pdf=1&item='+arr.join(':');
                else alert("尚未選擇購買商品！");  
            }
            function item_select(flag){
                $('input[name="C1"]').attr('checked',flag ? 'checked' : '');
                $(flag ? 'input[name="C1"]:checked' : 'input[name="C1"]').each(function(){
                    var div = $(this).parent().get(0);
                    var li = $(div).parent().get(0)
                    $(li).removeClass();
                    $(li).addClass(flag ? "item select" : "item");  
                });
            }
            function changePage(elm){
                var index = $(elm).val();
                window.location = "/exep/prod_search.php?cat=1&key=%E7%B6%B2%E8%B7%AF%E7%A8%8B%E5%BC%8F%E8%A8%AD%E8%A8%88&qsub=&qqsub=&page=" + index + "&sort=1&f=%3A%3A%3A%3A%3A%3A%3A%3A0%3A0%3A&c=";
            }
            function changeView(elm){
                window.location = "/exep/prod_search.php?cat=all&key=%E7%B6%B2%E8%B7%AF%E7%A8%8B%E5%BC%8F%E8%A8%AD%E8%A8%88&v=1";
            }
            function collapse(elm, type){
                window.location = "/exep/prod_search.php?cat=all&key=%E7%B6%B2%E8%B7%AF%E7%A8%8B%E5%BC%8F%E8%A8%AD%E8%A8%88&c=" + type + "&sort=1";
            }
            function advancedSearch(elm){
                var advancedForm = $("#advancedsearch");
                var rel = $(advancedForm).attr("rel");
                var key = encodeURI($("input[id='key'][name='key']").val());
                var catV = $("#query_type > option:selected").val();
                $(advancedForm).attr("action", "/exep/prod_search.php?cat=" + catV + "&key=" + key + "&c=&sort=1");
                var checked = $('#advancedsearch :checkbox').map(function() {
                	if($(this).attr('checked')) return 1;
                	else return 0;
				}).get(); 
                var price = [0, 0];
                if($.trim($('#price_min').val()).length) price[0] = $.trim($('#price_min').val());
                if($.trim($('#price_max').val()).length) price[1] = $.trim($('#price_max').val());
                var advancedList = $.merge(checked, price).join();
                 $.ajax({
                    type: 'get',
                    url: 'http://search.books.com.tw/exep/prod_search_mining.php',
                    data: 'area=' + rel + '&ref=' + act + '&adlist=' + advancedList,
                    error: function(data) {$(advancedForm).submit();},
                    success: function(data) {$(advancedForm).submit();}
                }); 
            }
            function reSearch(elm) {
                var fm = 0, bfm = 1, val = [];
                if($(elm).attr("id") == "fuzzySearch") fm = 1, bfm = 2;
                $("input[name='userTerm[]']:checked").each(function(i){
                    val[i] = $("label[for='" + $(this).attr('id') + "']").text();
                });
                if($.trim($("#customSearchText").val()) != '' && $.trim($("#customSearchText").val()) != "請輸入其它關鍵字") val.push($.trim($("#customSearchText").val()));
                if(val.length > 0) window.location = '/exep/prod_search.php?fm=' + fm + '&bfm=' + bfm + '&key=' + val.join(' ');
                else alert("請選擇關鍵字！");
            }

            function switch_li_bg(elm){
                var div = $(elm).parent().get(0);
                var li = $(div).parent().get(0)
                $(li).removeClass();
                if(elm.checked) $(li).addClass("item select");
                else $(li).addClass("item"); 
            }
            var s = '130';
            function item_compare(){
                var arr = new Array;
                $('input[name="C1"]:checked').each(function(){
                    arr.push(this.value);
                });
                if(arr.length > 0) window.open('http://search.books.com.tw/exep/prod_search_redir.php?key=%E7%B6%B2%E8%B7%AF%E7%A8%8B%E5%BC%8F%E8%A8%AD%E8%A8%88&area=mid_cmp&page=3&type=cmp&item='+arr.join(':'), 'wp1');
                else alert("尚未選擇商品！"); 
            }
            function item_putcart(){
                var arr = new Array;
                $('input[name="C1"]:checked').each(function(){
                    arr.push(this.value);
                });
                if(arr.length > 0) window.location = 'http://search.books.com.tw/exep/prod_search_redir.php?key=%E7%B6%B2%E8%B7%AF%E7%A8%8B%E5%BC%8F%E8%A8%AD%E8%A8%88&area=mid_cart&page=3&cart=1&pdf=1&item='+arr.join(':');
                else alert("尚未選擇購買商品！");  
            }
            function item_select(flag){
                $('input[name="C1"]').attr('checked',flag ? 'checked' : '');
                $(flag ? 'input[name="C1"]:checked' : 'input[name="C1"]').each(function(){
                    var div = $(this).parent().get(0);
                    var li = $(div).parent().get(0)
                    $(li).removeClass();
                    $(li).addClass(flag ? "item select" : "item");  
                });
            }
            function changePage(elm){
                var index = $(elm).val();
                window.location = "/exep/prod_search.php?cat=1&key=%E7%B6%B2%E8%B7%AF%E7%A8%8B%E5%BC%8F%E8%A8%AD%E8%A8%88&qsub=&qqsub=&page=" + index + "&sort=1&f=%3A%3A%3A%3A%3A%3A%3A%3A0%3A0%3A&c=";
            }
            function changeView(elm){
                window.location = "/exep/prod_search.php?cat=all&key=%E7%B6%B2%E8%B7%AF%E7%A8%8B%E5%BC%8F%E8%A8%AD%E8%A8%88&v=1";
            }
            function collapse(elm, type){
                window.location = "/exep/prod_search.php?cat=all&key=%E7%B6%B2%E8%B7%AF%E7%A8%8B%E5%BC%8F%E8%A8%AD%E8%A8%88&c=" + type + "&sort=1";
            }
            function advancedSearch(elm){
                var advancedForm = $("#advancedsearch");
                var rel = $(advancedForm).attr("rel");
                var key = encodeURI($("input[id='key'][name='key']").val());
                var catV = $("#query_type > option:selected").val();
                $(advancedForm).attr("action", "/exep/prod_search.php?cat=" + catV + "&key=" + key + "&c=&sort=1");
                var checked = $('#advancedsearch :checkbox').map(function() {
                	if($(this).attr('checked')) return 1;
                	else return 0;
				}).get(); 
                var price = [0, 0];
                if($.trim($('#price_min').val()).length) price[0] = $.trim($('#price_min').val());
                if($.trim($('#price_max').val()).length) price[1] = $.trim($('#price_max').val());
                var advancedList = $.merge(checked, price).join();
                 $.ajax({
                    type: 'get',
                    url: 'http://search.books.com.tw/exep/prod_search_mining.php',
                    data: 'area=' + rel + '&ref=' + act + '&adlist=' + advancedList,
                    error: function(data) {$(advancedForm).submit();},
                    success: function(data) {$(advancedForm).submit();}
                }); 
            }
            function reSearch(elm) {
                var fm = 0, bfm = 1, val = [];
                if($(elm).attr("id") == "fuzzySearch") fm = 1, bfm = 2;
                $("input[name='userTerm[]']:checked").each(function(i){
                    val[i] = $("label[for='" + $(this).attr('id') + "']").text();
                });
                if($.trim($("#customSearchText").val()) != '' && $.trim($("#customSearchText").val()) != "請輸入其它關鍵字") val.push($.trim($("#customSearchText").val()));
                if(val.length > 0) window.location = '/exep/prod_search.php?fm=' + fm + '&bfm=' + bfm + '&key=' + val.join(' ');
                else alert("請選擇關鍵字！");
            }

                if("all" != "1") {
